 Know several important facts related to Labor Day 1
 majdoor diwas kii shuruyaat canada main 1972 main hui
 It was started to demand the rights of workers
 2
 Labor Day was celebrated for the first time on 5 September 1882 in America as a celebration
 is avasar par mazdooron ne bhaashan die
 3
 duniya ke kai deshon main majdoor diwas 'may de' ke rup main manaaya jaataa he
 It started in Chicago
 mazdooron ne vahaan maang kii ki ve sirf 8 ghante kaam karenge
 For this he campaigned, went on strike and performed
 4
 It is not yet known who was the founder of Labor Day

, the founder of the American Federation of Labor
 mcguri ne isaki shuruyaat kii thi

 5

 haalanki anya sitaron ne is maamle main chinmayi kii tarah suchithra kaa saath nahin diya
 Actor-director p Samutirakani tweeted, "somebody needs mental improvement and treatment
 abhinaytaon or abhinetriyon ke naam or izzat ko nuksaan pahunchane kii anaavashyak koshish
 Use social media properly
 "tippaniyan 10
 south indian artist association ke adhyaksh abhinayta vishaal ne kaha, " jo video or photo post kiye gaye hai ve phek hai
 We are finding out who uploaded them
 suchithra kaa ilaaj chal rahaa he
 " dhanush ne haal hi main film power pandi kii shooting samaapt kii he, unhone is film kaa nirdesan kiya he
 These days he is busy shooting for VIP 2, directed by his sister-in-law and Rajinikanth's daughter Soundarya
 is film main abhinetri kaajol bhi mahatvapurn bhoomika nibhaa rahi hai
 1
 farvari ke ant main suchithra ke twitor handle se unke haath main ai ek kharonch kii photo post kii gai
 In this tweet, Dhanush's security guards were accused of misbehaving with Suchitra
 unhone twit main likhaa, "main suchi hum, main waapas aa gai
 i am safe and want to tell everyone how dirty game Dhanush has played
 " iske baad pichley saptaah abhinaytaon kii kai vyaktigat tasviren suchithra ke twitor handle se # Suchileaks hashtag ke saath post kii gayi
 These included photographs of Dhanush, Trisha Krishnan, RJ Chinmayi and Hansika Motwani
 2
 These pictures were later deleted and in conversation with a TV channel, Suchitra said, "my Twitter account has been hacked and i did not know that private pictures of stars have been shared on my page
 shuukravaar subah dhanush kii dost aditi ravichandran ne mujhe is bare main jaankaree di
 i have hired a private investigator to investigate the matter
 " baad main kuch or tasviren share kii gayi
 3
 kuch twits main suchithra ne paroksh rup se apane saathiyon par casting couch kaa bhi aarope lagaaya
 4
 suchithra ke pati karthik, jo ek stand ap kamedian or abhinayta hai, ne apane fasebuk pej par ek video post karte hue kaha ki acount hack nahin hua he
 He said, "it shows what emotional state he is in and all of us in the family are doing everything possible to overcome him
" " unhone media se guzarish kii ki ve suchithra ko vaise treet karen jaise parivaar ke kisi sadsy ko kiya jaataa he
 The video was later removed
 5
 In place of this video of Karthik, a post was shared on his Facebook page in which he said, "as a family, the last few days were very difficult for us as Suchitra's Twitter account was hacked
 aaj hamane unka acount ritrive kar liya he
 He did not make any tweets from his account in the last few days and they were completely wrong
 main samajhataa hum ki isse jude logon ko un twits kii vajah se pareshaaniyon kaa saamana karnaa padaa or main vyaktigat rup se unase is baat ke liye maafee maangata hum
 i request the media to show sensitivity and not sensationalize the matter
 aap sabhi ke sahyog ke liye shukriya
 " 6
 Speaking to a Tamil channel, Suchitra claimed that she and Karthik were getting divorced and were taken to the hospital without her consent
 unhone kaha, "karthik bahut achche insaan hai
 They have the qualities of Lord Rama
 main jaanati hum ki ham talaak le rahe hai
 It is sad for all the people associated with it, but we are doing it because of problems that are not solved
 main aspataal main thi
 i was forced to the hospital
 " 7
 superstar rajnikant ke damaad dhanush ne suchithra ke twit par ab tak koi pratikriya nahin di he
 But her sister Vimala Geeta did a post on Facebook in this regard, which wrote, "twitter has become a medium where anyone can say anything, post anything
 yah dekhnaa dukhad he ki ek aise plateform par jahaan 12 saal ke bacchon kaa bhi acount he, phek porn video post kiye jate hai
 And the worst is that people demand such videos
 " unhone ab apane sabhi soshal media acount dactivet kar liye hai
 8
 gayika chinmayi shripada kii tasviren bhi # Suchileaks ke tahat post kii gai thim
 She informed several tweets one by one that Suchitra's husband Karthik told them that Suchitra's condition was not good and she was going through an emotional phase
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki suchithra ke acount main jo kuch bhi chal rahaa he vah galat he
 He also wrote that Suchitra has blocked him and his conscience is clear
 9
 However, other stars did not support Suchitra like Chinmayi in this matter
 abhinayta-nirdeshak pi samutiraqni ne twit kiya, "kisi ko maansik sudhaar or ilaaj kii jarurat he
 Unnecessary attempts to harm the name and respect of actors and actresses
 soshal media kaa sahi istemaal karen
 "comments 10
 Actor Vishal, president of the South Indian Artists Association, said, “the videos and photos posted are fake
 ham pataa laga rahe hai ki inhen kisne aplod kiya he
 Suchitra is undergoing treatment
 " Dhanush has recently finished shooting for the film Power Pindi, he directed this film
 in dinon vah apni saali or rajnikant kii beti saundarya ke nirdesan main ban rahi viipi 2 kii shooting main vyast hai

 5
 karthik ke is video kii jagah unke fasebuk pej par ek post share kiya gaya jisamen unhone kaha, "parivaar ke taur par pichley kuch din hamaare liye kaaphi mushkil rahe kyonki suchithra kaa twitor acount hack kar diya gaya tha

 pichley kuch dinon main unke acount se jo bhi twit kiye gaye vah unhone nahin kiye the or ve puri tarah galat the

 main media se guzarish karata hum ki samvedansheeltaa dikhaaen or is maamle ko sansanikhej na banaaen
 Thanks for all of your cooperation
 " 6
 ek tamil channel se baat karte hue suchithra ne daawa kiya ki unka or karthik kaa talaak ho rahaa he or unki marji ke bina unhen aspataal le jaaya gaya tha

 unamem bhagwaan ram ke gun hai

 a very shocking case of honor killing has come up in Shahjahanpur, UP
 do sage bhaaiyon ne kathith taur par apni bahan ke sir ko dhad se alag kar diya or sir lekar faraar ho gaye
 They did so because she allegedly went to meet her boyfriend
 is ghatana ke baad se ilaake main dehshat faili hui he
 The police have taken the dead body and are searching for both the brothers
 tippaniyan The 18-year-old sister of these two brothers living in Bawni Chowki village reportedly fell in love with a boy and wanted to marry him
 isko lekar donon bhai naaraaz the
 Allegedly on Tuesday, when she ran away from the house and went to the boy's house, the two brothers forcibly brought him from there to the village chaupal and beheaded him
 iske baad se ve faraar hai
 In Bawni Chowki village under police station Parour, the head of the younger sister was severed from her torso at once
 ve use kathith taur par peetate hue chaoupal tak lekar aae
 The police is investigating the case and is investigating
 baavnee chaowkee gaanv main rahane vaale in donon bhaaiyon kii 18 saal kii bahan kathith taur par kisi ladke se pyaar karti thi or usase shaadi karnaa chaahati thi
 Both brothers were angry about this
 kathith taur par mangalvaar ko jab vah ghar se bhagkar us ladke ke ghar chali gai, tab donon bhai usko vahaan se jabaran gaanv kii chaoupal main le aae or uskaa sir kaat diya

[endif] pradhanmantri narendra modi kaa intervyuu lene se pehle abhinayta akshay kumaar ne spasht kiya tha ki yah ek gaiyr-raajnneetik intervyuu he
 From the first question, he also proved that his intention is not to do political questions and answers at all
 pehla sawaal akshay kumaar ne apane driver kii beti kaa hawala dete hue poocha, kya hamaare pradhanmantri aam khate hai, khate hai to kaise-katkar yaa phir guthli ke saath khate hai? pradhanmantri ne halke phulke andaaj main jawaab bhi diya
 But as the interview progressed, political talk became involved
 haalanki pradhanmantri ne jaanboojhkar siyaasi baaten kii yaa aam baton par siyasat hone lagi, yah spasht taur par kahana shaayad mushkil he
 Here are some questions asked during the interview and their answers, which were accused of being political - on Akshay Kumar's question whether you get angry
 ise rokane ke liye kya karte hai, aapaki chhavi kahin na kahin strict adminester kii he?modi jawaab dete hai- chaparasi se lekar adhikari tak mujhe kabhi bhi gussa vyakt karne kaa mauka nahin aayaa
 Being strict is a different thing
 lekin main gusse kii jagah logon ko prerit karata hum kaam karne ke liye
 i act like a helping hand
 
 
 
 i learn from people and also teach
 junior afasaron ko chutkule sunaata rahata hum
 a joke as well - "I had gone to Pune, i had to go to the Sangh's office there
" to main paidal-paidal chal rahaa tha, ek auto vaala mere peeche lagaataar chal rahaa tha
 Asked him, brother, why are you coming with me? usne kaha aap baithenge nahin isamen! maine kaha nahin, to usne kaha aap samaajawaadee nahin ho? maine poocha kyon to usne kaha, samaajawaadee janata ko dikhaane ke liye bheed main kabhi auto main nahin baithte lekin ekant main fouran baith jate hai
 i asked, why so? Because they show themselves hardworking
 ''raajnneeti kuch yun hui -darasal aksar yah baat uthati rahati he ki narendra modi jab mantriyon adhikariyon kii meeting lete hai to ve kisi kii sunate nahin, daant-fatkaar lagaate hai
 Mobile switches off completely
 intervyuu ko raajnneeti se prerit bataane vaale logon kaa maananaa he ki is sawaal ke jawaab ke jariye pradhanmantri ne is dharna ko todane kii koshish kii
 Not only this, the Samajwadi Party was also accused of directly targeting
 -akshay ke ek sawaal ke jawaab main pradhanmantri narendra modi ne batayaki pa
 Bengal Chief Minister Mamata Banerjee also sends him a couple of kurtas and sweets a year
 raajnneeti kuch yun hui-pashchim bengal par bhartiya janata party kii tirchhi najar he
 All efforts were made to conduct "mamata vs Modi" elections
 ab jahaan voter mamata or modi ko ek duusare kaa pratidwandi maan rahe hai vahaan jab 'didi' ke voter jab ye sunenge ki ve pradhanmantri narendra modi ko kurte or mithaiyaan bhejti hai to kya unke voter hataash honge
 The second speculation was that Modi gave a hint of an alliance of 'trin Mool Congress' after the election
 -yaheen nahin ruke naredra modi baraak obama se unke sambandh langotiya yaar kii tarah darshaate hue yah tak bataa daalaa kii vah ek duusare se 'tu' kahkar baat karte hai
 Politics became a joke - but it was also said that Narendra Modi had a close relationship with the former President of America
 yani videshon main modi ne apane desh kii chhavi aisi banaai ki america jaise desh kaa us samay kaa raashtrapati unhen apana behad kareebi dost maanane laga
 - Also mentioned the time of sleeping
 unhone kaha, obama bhi unase poochhate hai ki unhone sone kaa samay badhaayaa yaa nahin? itnaa hi nahin vyastata itani kii maa ko bhi samay nahin de pate
 We do not send money and money to mother
 raajnneeti kuch yun hui-ek-ek kshan desh seva main, apane oonche ohade kaa phayda maa ko bhi nahin pahunchaate
 -gulma also mentioned a meeting with Nabi Azad
 modi kehete hai, ''aaazaad or main gappe maar rahe the
 The media said, "hey you guys in such a friendly way?" So Ghulam Nabi Azad gave a very good answer, Look brother, what you think is not so
 ek family ke rup main ham log jitna jude hai uski aap log kalpana bhi nahin kar sakate ho
 "politics is something like this - even political parties or leaders who abuse Modi do not consider him an enemy
 kayaas to yahaan tak lage ki kya gulam nabi aaazaad nikat bhavishya main bhaajapai ho jaaenge?darasal is gaiyr-raajnneetik intervyuu ke jariye pradhanmantri narendra modi ne byopic par bain kii bharpai bhi kar lee
 They had to tell before the election that they live a very simple and simple life
 ve parivaarwaad se koson dur hai
 Do not use your position to benefit even the mother
 virdohi jahaan ise narendra modi kii raajnneetik chaal bataa rahe hai to vahiin samarthak unki chaturaai par virodhiyon kii chutki le rahe hai

 Lenovo's smartphone has a lot of great features, including Amazon's Alexa voice assistant and dual rear camera
 company ne isaki keemat EUR 399 (lagbhag 30,300 rupee) rakhi he
 Single SIM Moto X4 out of the box Android 7
 1 nugat par chalata he
 5 with Corning Glass Protection in it
 2-inch phul-hd (1080x1920 picksal) LTPS IPS disple diya gaya he
 This smartphone has 3 GB RAM and 2 with Adreno 508 GPU
 2ghz kwalkom snapadragon 630 octa kor procesar diya gaya he
 The internal storage of this smartphone is 32GB which can be increased to 2TB with the help of a card
 kuch aria main ise 4GB / 64GB opshan main bhi pesh kiya ja saktaa he
 Talking about the section of the camera, f / 2 in its rear
 0 aparchar vaala ek 12 megapixl kaa camera or f / 2
 a second 8 megapixel wide angle camera with 2 apertures has been given

 ' Life is punctuated with a series of memorable moments: your first day at the workplace, the day you get married, that moment when you hold your baby in your arms, the day when your child graduates, your retirement day
 
 
 the list is endless
 We need to be financially prepared at each phase to ensure that we can enjoy each of these special moments in life without much worry
 To ensure you are prepared for all life stage requirements and ensure your family is well protected in case of unforeseen circumstances, one needs life insurance plans that help you your future well and also provide protection to your loved ones
 Depending on the type of life insurance policy you choose, you can build a corpus for life's important milestones such as children's birth, education, marriage, plan for your post-retirement years
 What also is of paramount importance is to secure your family's financial future, should anything unfortunate were to happen
 The earlier you factor in life insurance in your financial planning, the better it is
 Here's how insurance can benefit you at every stage of life
 Unmarried young adults: You have just passed out of college and got yourself a dream job that promises you a fat pay cheque
 This is the time you should not lose sight of your goals
 You must judiciously plan your finances in such a way that apart from securing your present, you're covered for the future too
 Life insurance lets you do just that
 It acts as a safety net in times of crisis
 Once you are married, it will help you secure the future of your spouse and children
 The biggest advantage of life insurance is that it is financially beneficial in the long run
 The younger you are when you buy insurance, the more affordable your premium will be
 Not to forget the tax benefits that you can avail through a life insurance policy
 Newly married: The very thought of sharing your life with a loved one is exciting and that's what makes marriage so special
 It is only natural then that you would want to lead a secure and comfortable life with your spouse
 In the wake of additional expenses and responsibilities that marriage brings along, it is necessary to make changes to your financial plan
 a life insurance policy can go a long way in securing the financial future of your family
 From providing regular returns during your lifetime to taking care of your family's financial needs in case of any eventuality, life insurance has multifold benefits
 Married with kids:parenthood marks the beginning of a wonderful phase in any person's life
 Your world revolves around your child and you would want the best for him or her
 You follow every growth milestone of your child with love and fondness
 During this exciting phase, somewhere at the back of your mind, you also keep thinking about the future of your child - school, college, higher studies and even marriage
 You think of ways you can prepare yourself financially to meet all these requirements
 Choosing the right life insurance plan will simplify things for you
 As a new parent, you can build a corpus over a period of time for your kids' education and marriage
 Likewise, in the case of any unfortunate event, the insurance amount will ensure that the future of your children is not negatively impacted and they can fulfill all their dreams
 retirees:years roll by
 While your children have settled down and are now busy with their own lives, you are all set to enter the most interesting phase of your life - the post-retirement period
 Gone are the days when retirement meant idling away reading newspapers while sipping tea
 These days, retirees look forward to making the most of the golden period of their lives
 Be it holidays around the world or trying their hand at new activities, they want to live their lives to the fullest
 And for all this, parents wouldn't want to financially depend on their children
 Opting for a life insurance plan, that offers retirement solutions, early on in life will be of great help during your retirement years
 It will help you lead a comfortable post-retirement life
 Besides, old age is often characterized by fragile health
 As a result, there can be many unplanned expenses too
 Your insurance policy will provide for those as well
 Now that you have identified yourself as part of one of the above groups, make sure you choose the right life insurance policy
 Protecting you for lifefrom affordable term insurance plans to monthly income plans,bharti AXA Lifehas solutions that suit you irrespective of the group you belong to
 Their insurance plans are designed to financially protect you and your family
 The company also offers an online term insurance plan for those who wish to directly buy a policy
 You also understand that this relationship is long-term and a key point of expectation is the claims management process
 At the time of claims settlement,bharti AXA Lifeprovides you services of dedicated claims handler who will help with the claims process
 From explaining the finer points to assisting with paperwork, the claims handler will be with the beneficiary throughout
 This will not only quicken the claims process, but also lend a personal touch to it
 This way, with life insurance, you can meet all your financial goals at different life-stages and also secure your family's future

 mysore ke aitihaasik amba vila pales main yah shahi shaadi hui
 The marriage took place after 40 years in the Royal House of Mysore
 shaadi kii rasmen ravivaar se yaduvir dwaara raajaguru kii pad puja rasm ke saath shuru ho gai thi
 Yaduvir studied from Boston and is only 24 years old
 trishika duungarpur (rajasthan) ke raja harshavardhan singh or rani maheshri kumari kii beti hai
 She recently returned from the US
 pichley saal 28 may ko rajgaraane kii parampara ke anusaar yaduvir kaa rajgaraane ke mukhiya ke taur par rajtilak kiya gaya tha

 shaadi kaa resepshan 28 june ko mysore or 2 july ko bengaluru main diya jayega

 tippaniyan The last descendant of the Wadair royal family was Srikantadatta Narasimharaja Wadair

 wadere vansh ne mysore main 1399 se 1947 tak shashan kiya
